\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01154}01154\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Best\ possible\ score\ is\ 1.0\ and\ it\ can\ be\ negative\ (because\ the}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01156}01156\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ non-\/constant,\ a\ constant\ model\ that\ always\ predicts\ the\ average\ y}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01157}01157\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ disregarding\ the\ input\ features\ would\ get\ a\ :math:\`{}R\string^2\`{}\ score\ of\ 0.0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01158}01158\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01159}01159\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ In\ the\ particular\ case\ when\ \`{}\`{}y\_true\`{}\`{}\ is\ constant,\ the\ :math:\`{}R\string^2\`{}\ score}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01160}01160\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ is\ not\ finite:\ it\ is\ either\ \`{}\`{}NaN\`{}\`{}\ (perfect\ predictions)\ or\ \`{}\`{}-\/Inf\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01161}01161\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ (imperfect\ predictions).\ To\ prevent\ such\ non-\/finite\ numbers\ to\ pollute}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01162}01162\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ higher-\/level\ experiments\ such\ as\ a\ grid\ search\ cross-\/validation,\ by\ default}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01163}01163\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ these\ cases\ are\ replaced\ with\ 1.0\ (perfect\ predictions)\ or\ 0.0\ (imperfect}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{metrics_2__regression_8py_source_l01164}01164\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ predictions)\ respectively.\ You\ can\ set\ \`{}\`{}force\_finite\`{}\`{}\ to\ \`{}\`{}False\`{}\`{}\ to}}
